***hoeven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a> (1106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. Cognates are attested much more sparsely, and <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>, than those of the prefixed form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></i>. It therefore appears that <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be necessary</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to, to have to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeft.html>hoeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoeken.html>zoeken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>have to</b> seek far.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeft.html>hoeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vragen.html>vragen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You only <b>need to</b> ask it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I only <b>need</b> two (of them).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to urinate or defecate, to need to go</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Whenever a finite form of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></i> introduces a verb phrase, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inserted before the first verb in the verb phrase.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hufą</i>.

***hoi.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a> (515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly a spontaneous alteration of the interjection <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>ho</a></i>. The use as a joyful exclamation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attested from the 16th century; use as an informal greeting appears only in the 20th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A greeting acknowledging someone’s arrival or presence, comparable to English <a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>hey</a>, hi
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>Hoi</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>?</i> — <a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, how's it going?</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An exclamation of joy.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tante.html>tante</a> in Marokko <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a>, hiep <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have an aunt in Morocco and she's coming <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, yippee <b>yay</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:goedendag.html>goedendag</a></li>

***hok.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hok.html>hok</a> (8653)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hok.html>hok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hokken.html>hokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hokje.html>hokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A living shelter for domesticated animals such as a kennel, cage, <a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a> or a <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a>.</li>
<li>A closet or small room.</li>
<li>A den; a small and often dark dwelling such as a <a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>.</li></ol>

***hol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a> (4487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holen.html>holen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holletje.html>holletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hole, hollow, cavity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cargo hold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href = vnd.unilang:anus.html>anus</a>, arsehole; both anatomical senses of butt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zul.html>zul</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoonmaken.html>schoonmaken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> have to clean up your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b> yourself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any other bodily cavity that resembles a hole</li>
<li>An artificial opening such as a slit</li>
<li>burrow (a hole or <a href = vnd.unilang:tunnel.html>tunnel</a> dug by a small animal, like a rabbit, used as a dwelling)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unsanitary and/or unpleasant place; shithole</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">hole</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gat.html>gat</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">opening</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:holbewoner.html>holbewoner</a> (32592)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewoner.html>bewoner</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holbewoner.html>holbewoner</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holbewoners.html>holbewoners</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holbewoner.html>holbewonertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a> (4601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holie</i>, a shortened variation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holyn</i> (gt; English dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hollen.html>hollen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">holm</i>), from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">holeġn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:holen.html>holen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a>; prince, protector</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulisaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">butcher's broom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱol-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn, awn; a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of thorny plant; prickly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">holin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">hollin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">holyn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hulst.html>hulst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hulst.html>Hulst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">houx</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"<a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a>" lt; Germanic</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hylver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Welsh <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">celyn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ко́лос</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kólos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ear of wheat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Albanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">kalli</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straw, chaff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">culmus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stalk, <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Sanskrit <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कटम्ब</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaṭamba</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">класъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klasŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ear of grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hollies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various shrubs or (mostly) small trees, of the genus <i>Ilex</i>, either evergreen or deciduous, used as decoration especially at Christmas.</li>
<li>The wood from this tree.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a qualifier</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several unrelated plant species likened to <i>Ilex</i> because of their prickly, evergreen foliage and/or round, bright-red berries</li></ol>
</body>

***homeopathie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathie</a> (75376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">homeopathy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">homéopathie</i>, etc.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Homeopathy</span>: a pseudomedical method invented by Hahnemann based on analogies between symptoms and <a href = vnd.unilang:remedies.html>remedies</a>, using extremely diluted <a href = vnd.unilang:doses.html>doses</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">homeopaat</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathisch.html>homeopathisch</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alternatieve.html>alternatieve</a> geneeswijze <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorspronkelijk.html>oorspronkelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geformuleerd.html>geformuleerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Samuel Hahnemann <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gepubliceerd.html>gepubliceerd</a> in 1796
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<b><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>Homeopathie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:effectiever.html>effectiever</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> placebo" <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">home</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">trainer</i>. A compound word coined by Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> using English component <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>. The compound does not exist in English, but does in German as <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hometrainer.html>Hometrainer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stationary bicycle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***homo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a> (1728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homoseksueel.html>homoseksueel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homootje.html>homootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neutral<span class="ib-comma">,</span> not offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gay, homosexual</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used as a general slur</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a general, neutral and somewhat informal term for a homosexual person. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a slur by some, but the term, or its use in this way, can be considered offensive. Because the word itself <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not inherently offensive or vulgar, some people may take offense at the implication that homosexuality <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> something negative and shameful that could be used as a derogatory term. This depends, of course, on a particular person's attitude towards homosexuality. Compare similar usage of English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gay</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a> <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderdeel.html>onderdeel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaste.html>vaste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbindingen.html>verbindingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontlenen.html>ontleend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latijn.html>Latijn</a>)</i></li>

***homunculus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:homunculus.html>homunculus</a> (54283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:homunculus.html>homunculus</a></i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">homō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:homunculus.html>homunculus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">homunculi</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A miniature <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, once imagined by spermists to be present in human sperm.</li>
<li>The nerve map of the human body that exists on the parietal lobe of the human brain.</li></ol>

***hond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> (544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hundaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱwn̥tós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱwṓ</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hund</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hound</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>honden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hondje.html>hondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dog, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:canis.html>Canis</a> lupus familiaris</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hundą</i>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honderd.html>honderd</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>honden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hondje.html>hondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an old unit of area measuring 100 <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeden.html>roeden</a></i>, approximately 0.14 <a href = vnd.unilang:hectares.html>hectares</a></li></ol>
<hr />

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hontsch</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog, hound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">denominative adjectival <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>honds</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>hondser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>honds</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">hondst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></i>) canine, relating to dogs</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>concerning humans</i>) currish, doggish, doggy, notably:
<ol><li>insolent, impertinent, shameless</li>
<li>rude, coarse, insulting</li></ol></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog, canine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dolheid.html>dolheid</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">madness, frenzy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:diergeneeskunde.html>diergeneeskunde</a>)</span> virusziekte <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>honden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorkomt.html>voorkomt</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>  <a href = vnd.unilang:vossen.html>vossen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:katten.html>katten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:apen.html>apen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vleermuizen.html>vleermuizen</a>)) <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beet.html>beet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overgedragen.html>overgedragen</a>.

***hongerig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a> (6476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hongerich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hungragaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hungrugaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hungry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honger.html>honger</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hungrig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hungry</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongeriger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">hongerigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hungry</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal Dutch expression for “I'm hungry” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:honger.html>honger</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I have hunger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> rather than the literal equivalent <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></i> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very uncommon.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a></b>
</p>
